        <div class="jive-rendered-content">
         <span>Hi,</span>
         <br>
         <br>
         <span>I was testing the search functionality in Share when it started hanging, resulting a few minutes later in a 503 error. I checked the logs and found the following error (repeated multiple times):</span>
         <br>
         <br>
         <pre class="language-none line-numbers"><code>2013-10-03 00:22:05,440&nbsp; WARN&nbsp; [solr.tracker.CoreTracker] [SolrTrackerScheduler_Worker-2] Tracking communication timed out.<span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <br>
         <br>
         <br>
         <span>Since I didn't know what was causing this timeout, I tried increasing the solr (</span>
         <pre class="language-none line-numbers"><code>solr.solrConnectTimeout=10000<span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <span>) and re-indexing the repository by following the walkthrough in the documentation, with no luck.</span>
         <br>
         <br>
         <span>If I restart the Alfresco service, Share is available again, but searching will trigger the 503 error and leave Share hanging once again.</span>
         <br>
         <br>
         <br>

            <div class="jive-comment-content clearfix">
             <a href="/people/rjohnson" title="rjohnson" class="j-avatar  jiveTT-hover-user" data-userid="112193"><img class="jive-avatar" src="https://community.alfresco.com/api/core/v3/people/112193/avatar?a=1374" data-username="rjohnson" height="72" data-height="72" width="72" data-random="47195073369089126" alt="rjohnson" title="rjohnson"></a>
             <div class="j-comment-header">
              <span class="jive-comment-meta font-color-meta-light"><span class="j-username-wrap"><a href="/people/rjohnson" data-username="rjohnson" data-userid="112193" class="jive-username-link  jiveTT-hover-user  ">rjohnson</a> </span><a href="#comment-677380" id="comment-modDate-677380" class="font-color-meta-light">Oct 5, 2013 6:31 PM</a></span>
             </div>
             <div class="j-mark-correct js-mark-correct  clearfix" style="display:none;">
              <a href="#" data-object-id="677380" data-object-type="2" data-command="mark" data-type="correct" class="js-action-link js-correct-answer-link js-mark-correct-answer"><span class=""></span>Mark Correct</a>
              <div class="j-marked-correct">
               <span class="jive-icon-glyph icon-star3"></span>Correct Answer
              </div>
             </div>
             <div id="comment-body-677380">
              <!-- [DocumentBodyStart:d411f087-73d0-4f32-8d47-adbec3284dd4] -->
              <div class="jive-rendered-content">
               <span>From your error log, the issue seems to be a timeout on AJP. This is a module that is often used in Apache to allow you to map https requests so that you not need to specify the port or "the application" to get to Alfresco (i.e. </span>
               <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmyhost.co.uk%3A8443%2Fshare" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://myhost.co.uk:8443/share</a>
               <span> becomes just </span>
               <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmyhost.co.uk" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://myhost.co.uk</a>
               <span>).</span>
               <br>
               <br>
               <span>As AJP is being moaned about, it occurs to me that you may have used the AJP module in Apache to do something and having changed alfresco.global messed up that mapping.</span>
               <br>
               <br>
              </div>
              <!-- [DocumentBodyEnd:d411f087-73d0-4f32-8d47-adbec3284dd4] -->

           <li class="reply j-anchor-target " id="comment-677383" data-object-type="2" data-object-id="677383">
            <div class="jive-comment-content clearfix">
             <a href="/people/michael.chen_rivetlogic" title="michael.chen_rivetlogic" class="j-avatar  jiveTT-hover-user" data-userid="104016"><img class="jive-avatar" src="https://community.alfresco.com/api/core/v3/people/104016/avatar?a=-1" data-username="michael.chen_rivetlogic" height="72" data-height="72" width="72" data-random="47195073364233902" alt="michael.chen_rivetlogic" title="michael.chen_rivetlogic"></a>
             <div class="j-comment-header">
              <span class="jive-comment-meta font-color-meta-light"><span class="j-username-wrap"><a href="/people/michael.chen_rivetlogic" data-username="michael.chen_rivetlogic" data-userid="104016" class="jive-username-link  jiveTT-hover-user  ">michael.chen_rivetlogic</a> </span><a href="#comment-677383" id="comment-modDate-677383" class="font-color-meta-light">Feb 1, 2014 5:55 AM</a></span>
             </div>
             <div class="j-mark-correct js-mark-correct  clearfix" style="display:none;">
              <a href="#" data-object-id="677383" data-object-type="2" data-command="mark" data-type="correct" class="js-action-link js-correct-answer-link js-mark-correct-answer"><span class=""></span>Mark Correct</a>
              <div class="j-marked-correct">
               <span class="jive-icon-glyph icon-star3"></span>Correct Answer
              </div>
             </div>
             <div id="comment-body-677383">
              <!-- [DocumentBodyStart:8b5f3064-138b-47de-b144-a8aea021fd11] -->
              <div class="jive-rendered-content">
               <span>Alex, your suspicion of connection timeout was correct, but the right setting is (after many many hours of trying):</span>
               <br>
               <br>
               <span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; alfresco.socketTimeout=160000</span>
               <br>
               <br>
               <span>in both of these files:</span>
               <br>
               <br>
               <span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; alf_data/solr/archive-SpacesStore/conf/solrcore.properties</span>
               <br>
               <span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; alf_data/solr/workspace-SpacesStore/conf/solrcore.properties</span>
               <br>
               <br>
               <span>Turns out this is because your machine is too slow, and during startup, the tracker threads seem to have been launched too early and exceeded the default 1 minute waiting for port 8443 to accept and start SSL handshake. The above setting added 100 seconds to the wait. I consider this an Alfresco bug.</span>
               <br>
              </div>
              <!-- [DocumentBodyEnd:8b5f3064-138b-47de-b144-a8aea021fd11] -->
             </div>

                <div class="jive-rendered-content">
                 <span>&lt;strong&gt;</span>
                 <br>
                 <span>2014-05-04 15:52:37,025 ERROR [extensions.webscripts.AbstractRuntime] [http-apr-8080-exec-13] Exception from executeScript - redirecting to status template error: nested exception is org.apache.ibatis.exceptions.TooManyResultsException: Expected one result (or null) to be returned by selectOne(), but found: 2</span>
                 <br>
                 <span>org.mybatis.spring.MyBatisSystemException: nested exception is org.apache.ibatis.exceptions.TooManyResultsException: Expected one result (or null) to be returned by selectOne(), but found: 2</span>
                 <br>
                 <span>&lt;/strong&gt;</span>
                 <br>
                 <br>
                 <br>
                 <span>It seems there are duplicated data in your database,you can check table "alf_content_url" to see if there are two records with the same value in column "content_url_short" and column "content_url_crc".</span>
                 <br>
                 <span>if it dose ,delete one record and corresponding data in table "alf_content_data" whose value in column "content_url_id" equals to id you delete in table "alf_content_url".</span>
                 <br>
                 <span>Make sure you do a backup before you do above operations</span>

                       <li class="reply j-anchor-target " id="comment-747849" data-object-type="2" data-object-id="747849">
                        <div class="jive-comment-content clearfix">
                         <a href="/people/bhuvan" title="bhuvan" class="j-avatar  jiveTT-hover-user" data-userid="78153"><img class="jive-avatar" src="https://community.alfresco.com/api/core/v3/people/78153/avatar?a=1005" data-username="bhuvan" height="72" data-height="72" width="72" data-random="47195073383319510" alt="bhuvan" title="bhuvan"></a>
                         <div class="j-comment-header">
                          <span class="jive-comment-meta font-color-meta-light"><span class="j-username-wrap"><a href="/people/bhuvan" data-username="bhuvan" data-userid="78153" class="jive-username-link  jiveTT-hover-user  ">bhuvan</a> </span>@ <a class="font-color-meta-light localScroll" href="#comment-747764" title="Go to message">kaynezhang</a> <small>on</small> <a href="#comment-747849" id="comment-modDate-747849" class="font-color-meta-light">Jun 7, 2014 4:52 PM</a></span>
                         </div>
                         <div class="j-mark-correct js-mark-correct  clearfix" style="display:none;">
                          <a href="#" data-object-id="747849" data-object-type="2" data-command="mark" data-type="correct" class="js-action-link js-correct-answer-link js-mark-correct-answer"><span class=""></span>Mark Correct</a>
                          <div class="j-marked-correct">
                           <span class="jive-icon-glyph icon-star3"></span>Correct Answer
                          </div>
                         </div>
                         <div id="comment-body-747849">
                          <!-- [DocumentBodyStart:8c618eee-e63f-4919-ada3-bbc273b91dcb] -->
                          <div class="jive-rendered-content">
                           <span>I am facing unable to login into share application by default but when I am placing dns url in share-security-config.xml I am able to login but </span>
                           <br>
                           <span>According to our client requirement they need two dns urls for WAN and Broadband urls but only one is working fine for share login how to enable two urls at a time. please help me any one.</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>Following is my code</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;config evaluator="string-compare" condition="CSRFPolicy" replace="true"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;!</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>Will be used and exposed to the client side code in Alfresco.contants.CSRF_POLICY.</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>Use the Alfresco.util.CSRFPolicy.getHeader() or Alfresco.util.CSRFPolicy.getParameter() with Alfresco.util.CSRFPolicy.getToken()</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>to set the token in custom 3rd party code.</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;client&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;cookie&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/cookie&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;header&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/header&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;parameter&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/parameter&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/client&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! The first rule with a matching request will get its action invoked, the remaining rules will be ignored. &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;filter&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;!</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>Certain Surf POST requests form the WebScript console must be allowed to pass without a token since</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>the Surf WebScript console code can't be dependent on a Share specific filter.</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;POST&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;path&gt;\/page\/caches\/dependency\/clear|\/page\/index|\/page\/surfBugStatus|\/page\/modules\/deploy|\/page\/modules\/module|\/page\/api\/javascript\/debugger&lt;/path&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertReferer"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertOrigin"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! Certain Share POST requests does NOT require a token &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;POST&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;path&gt;/page/dologin.*|\/page/site\/[^\/]+\/start-workflow|^\/page/start-workflow&lt;/path&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertReferer"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertOrigin"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! Clear the token when logging out &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;GET&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;path&gt;^/page/dologout.*&lt;/path&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="clearToken"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="session"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="cookie"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! Make sure the first token is generated &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="_alf_USER_ID"&gt;.*&lt;/attribute&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="Alfresco-CSRFToken"/&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! empty attribute element indicates null &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="generateToken"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="session"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="cookie"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! Refresh token on new "page" visit when a user is logged in &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;GET&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;path&gt;^/page/.*&lt;/path&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="_alf_USER_ID"&gt;.*&lt;/attribute&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="Alfresco-CSRFToken"&gt;.*&lt;/attribute&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="generateToken"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="session"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="cookie"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;! Verify multipart requests contains the token as a parameter and also correct referer &amp; origin header if available &gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;POST&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;header name="Content-Type"&gt;^multipart/.*&lt;/header&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="_alf_USER_ID"&gt;.*&lt;/attribute&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertToken"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="session"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="parameter"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertReferer"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertOrigin"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;!</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>Verify there is a token in the header for remaining state changing requests and also correct</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>referer &amp; origin headers if available. We "catch" all content types since just setting it to</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>"application/json.*" since a webscript that doesn't require a json request body otherwise would be</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>successfully executed using i.e. "text/plain".</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;method&gt;POST|PUT|DELETE&lt;/method&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;attribute name="_alf_USER_ID"&gt;.*&lt;/attribute&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/session&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/request&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertToken"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="session"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="header"&gt;Alfresco-CSRFToken&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertReferer"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="referer"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;action name="assertOrigin"&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="always"&gt;false&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdms.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dms.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;param name="origin"&gt;</span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdmspub.taashee.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://dmspub.taashee.com</a>
                           <span>&lt;/param&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/action&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/rule&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/filter&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <span>&lt;/config&gt;</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>I added two names like below but it is working only one.</span>
                           <br>
                           <br>
                           <span>I followed this link </span>
                           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=https%3A%2F%2Fissues.alfresco.com%2Fjira%2Fbrowse%2FALF-18175" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://issues.alfresco.com/jira/browse/ALF-18175</a>
